READY RECKONER
FEDERAL LAND TAX
I 1 or the purpose of assisting taxpayers to readily ascertain the
amount of tax payable by them under the Federal Land Tax Act 1910,
the accompanying Heady Reckoner Tables have been compiled at the
request of the Commonwealth Treasurer, under the direction of Mr.
G. H. Knibbs, C.M.G., F.R.S.S. It is hoped these tables will prove of
service to all persons concerned.
Federal Commissioner of Land Tax,
Melbourne, 7th February, 1911.

FEDERAL LAND TAX.
READY RECKONER FOR THE PURPOSE OF ASCERTAINING
THE AMOUNT OF TAX PAYABLE UNDER THE LAND TAX
ACT 1910 (No. 21) ON ANY GIVEN TAXABLE VALUE.
The first column represents a series of taxable values at intervals of �lOO,
and the second column (headed 0) gives the amount of tax payable thereon.
Each succeeding column gives the tax payable on the taxable value shown
in the first column plus the amount shown at the head of such succeeding
column, e.g. .'?Taxable value (for non-absentee) �5lO. Refer to Part I.
of Ready Reckoner. Find 500 in first column and then find the amount
stated against it in the column headed 10. The result is the tax payable
on a taxable value of �5lO.
To find the tax on �519, ascertain the tax on �5lO as before, and refer to
last column which shows the additional tax on each additional �1 of taxable
value at the rate applicable to the whole amount of taxable value.
